  <script>
    /*! loadCSS: load a CSS file asynchronously. [c]2016 @scottjehl, Filament Group, Inc. Licensed MIT */
    (function(w){
        "use strict";
        var loadCSS = function( href, before, media ){
            var doc = w.document;
            var ss = doc.createElement( "link" );
            var ref;
            if( before ){
                ref = before;
            }
            else {
                var refs = ( doc.body || doc.getElementsByTagName( "head" )[ 0 ] ).childNodes;
                ref = refs[ refs.length - 1];
            }

            var sheets = doc.styleSheets;
            ss.rel = "stylesheet";
            ss.href = href;
            ss.media = "only x";

            function ready( cb ){
                if( doc.body ){
                    return cb();
                }
                setTimeout(function(){
                    ready( cb );
                });
            }
            ready( function(){
                ref.parentNode.insertBefore( ss, ( before ? ref : ref.nextSibling ) );
            });
            var onloadcssdefined = function( cb ){
                var resolvedHref = ss.href;
                var i = sheets.length;
                while( i-- ){
                    if( sheets[ i ].href === resolvedHref ){
                        return cb();
                    }
                }
                setTimeout(function() {
                    onloadcssdefined( cb );
                });
            };

            function loadCB(){
                if( ss.addEventListener ){
                    ss.removeEventListener( "load", loadCB );
                }
                ss.media = media || "all";
            }
            if( ss.addEventListener ){
                ss.addEventListener( "load", loadCB);
            }
            ss.onloadcssdefined = onloadcssdefined;
            onloadcssdefined( loadCB );
            return ss;
        };
        if( typeof exports !== "undefined" ){
            exports.loadCSS = loadCSS;
        }
        else {
            w.loadCSS = loadCSS;
        }
    }( typeof global !== "undefined" ? global : this ));

    /*! CSS rel=preload polyfill. Depends on loadCSS function. [c]2016 @scottjehl, Filament Group, Inc. Licensed MIT  */
    (function( w ){
        if( !w.loadCSS ){
            return;
        }
        var rp = loadCSS.relpreload = {};
        rp.support = function(){
            try {
                return w.document.createElement( "link" ).relList.supports( "preload" );
            } catch (e) {
                return false;
            }
        };
        rp.poly = function(){
            var links = w.document.getElementsByTagName( "link" );
            for( var i = 0; i < links.length; i++ ){
                var link = links[ i ];
                if( link.rel === "preload" && link.getAttribute( "as" ) === "style" ){
                    w.loadCSS( link.href, link );
                    link.rel = null;
                }
            }
        };
        if( !rp.support() ){
            rp.poly();
            var run = w.setInterval( rp.poly, 300 );
            if( w.addEventListener ){
                w.addEventListener( "load", function(){
                    w.clearInterval( run );
                } );
            }
            if( w.attachEvent ){
                w.attachEvent( "onload", function(){
                    w.clearInterval( run );
                } )
            }
        }
    }( this ));

    /*! onloadCSS: adds onload support for asynchronous stylesheets loaded with loadCSS. [c]2016 @zachleat, Filament Group, Inc. Licensed MIT */    /* global navigator */
    function onloadCSS( ss, callback ) {
        var called;
        function newcb(){
            if( !called && callback ){
                called = true;
                callback.call( ss );
            }
        }
        if( ss.addEventListener ){
            ss.addEventListener( "load", newcb );
        }
        if( ss.attachEvent ){
            ss.attachEvent( "onload", newcb );
        }
        if( "isApplicationInstalled" in navigator && "onloadcssdefined" in ss ) {
            ss.onloadcssdefined( newcb );
        }
    }
</script>

      <h2 class="promotion--headline" style="color: #ff5b02">Why book with us?</h2> 
      <div class="promotion--blockContainer"> 
       <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-4"> 
        <h3 class="promotion--subheadline" style="color:#000">LUXURY 5 STAR TO VALUE 3 STAR</h3> 
        <div class="promotion--text"> 
         <p>Weve got beach holidays, city breaks and ski deals including flights and specially selected accommodation to suit you. Whether its a cheap holiday or luxury escape, a boutique hotel or a big name brand; our holidays ensure the best value for your money.</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-4"> 
        <h3 class="promotion--subheadline" style="color:#333333">PRICE MATCH GUARANTEE</h3> 
        <div class="promotion--text"> 
         <p style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: helvetica, arial, verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;"><font face="helvetica, arial, verdana, sans-serif" style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-size: 13px;">Find the same flight and hotel for a lower price elsewhere and we will match it  PLUS give you an extra £10 off (</span></font><a href="https://www.easyjet.com/en/holidays/info/price-match-guarantee">T&amp;Cs apply</a><font face="helvetica, arial, verdana, sans-serif" style="font-size: 12px;"><span style="font-size: 13px;">)</span></font><br></p>
         <p><font face="helvetica, arial, verdana, sans-serif"><span style="font-size: 13px;">Elements of your package price update every 15 minutes. The price therefore, may change during the booking process to reflect this. You will be notified should this happen.</span><br></font></p> 
        </div> 
       </div>
